<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Klassiker</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klassiek.html>klassiek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:classical.html>classical</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sports.html>sports</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>originally</a> Belgian <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> derives <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">classique</i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clêet</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klēth</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klaiþą</i>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kleid</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleed.html>Kleed</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cloth.html>cloth</a></i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleden.html>kleden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dress.html>dress</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:room.html>room</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cledermakere</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:loss.html>loss</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> intervocalic <i>-d-</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kleer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">singular <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> plurale tantum <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kleren.html>kleren</a></i></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maker.html>maker</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***kleingeestig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleingeestig.html>kleingeestig</a> (47096)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:mid.html>Mid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:late.html>late</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eighteenth.html>eighteenth</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:small.html>small</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geest.html>geest</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mind.html>mind</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>, calque <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a>  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kleingeistig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleingeestig.html>kleingeestig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleingeestig.html>kleingeestiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">kleingeestigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>narrow-minded, prejudiced
<ul><li><b>1788</b>, Elisabeth <a href = vnd.unilang:maria.html>Maria</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:post.html>Post</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brieven.html>brieven</a></i>, publ. <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:johannes.html>Johannes</a> Allart (<a href = vnd.unilang:third.html>third</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:print.html>print</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:page.html>page</a> 72.
